I absolutely love how there's no favoritism in STAYC. Line distributions and MV screen time are always fair and equitable. In all of their title tracks every member gets to have their own memorable part. Almost equal amount of contents, if one gets a vlog everyone else gets a vlog too, if one gets a cover everyone else gets a cover too. Recently Yoon has been getting more shows and contents but that is because she is their designated variety expert. Everyone's styled equally, they're always making sure that they all shines. In everything they are always arranged or listed by age. No single member is always in the center, when they are in a group formation or standing in a row they are always arranged either by age or height-based arrangement. On sns posts it's always equal amounts too. Even with the fans, every member's individual fandom are almost of the same size. They are so unlike basically every other kpop group where it is always just one or two members and the rest are just like backups or filler members.

HELLO SEEUN'S FIT ATE SO BAD
to give some honest feedback, i don't quite like this "silly" concept and sound stayc have going on atm. as someone who's followed their music since their debut, it's disappointing because their first four releases were so solid and had this "trendy" sound while still being diverse in concepts. beautiful monster was where i started sensing a shift in their sound but i didn't mind it because the song was still great. teddy bear though was a major let down for me. i don't mean this in a hateful way whatsover but it feels like they went from doing expensive and trendy sounding songs to repetitive silly/childish songs. i'm aware they got really great results from teddy bear and poppy, so i know this type of sound works well for them. its great for challenges and going viral but it just really isn't my cup of tea. personally i really hope they'll go back to their initial sound and do something more "serious" because i feel like that suits them the best. anyways, that being said, i don't consider bubble a bad song. the melody is fine (especially the chorus) but they definitely could have done a better job with the english lyrics. iffy yo iffy yeah, hello hello punch you like a 808, stupid stop.. no offense but these sound like they were written by a 10 year old. still, i rlly liked seeun's part in the bridge. the ì‚¬ë¼ì§ˆ ê±°í’ˆì¸ê±¸ ë„ˆë¬´ í”ë“¤ë¦¬ì§€ë§ˆ lyric is beautiful ğŸ«¶ğŸ»ğŸ«¶ğŸ» also, the girls looked pretty cute and sang very well, they seem to have improved a lot and in that sense their hard work definitely shows. i truly wish them all the best for the promotions <3 looking forward to seeing them on music shows soon !!
